#######################################################
# PRE-NORMAN INVASION - (Died on or before 1167.1.1)
#######################################################
#	Insular Christianity is applied for almost everyone in this date bracket.
##	The main exceptions are the Ivarings of Dublin after they naturalise to Irish, who remain Catholic. Diarmait mac Donnchad & his son Murchad (plus his other child & his grandkids) are also Catholic. This is mostly to represent Diarmait's extensive links and dealings with wider Britain, and to encourage the survival of Catholics in Meath & Leinster in 1066.
##	Plus a bunch of generic pagans in the very old files.
